Finish Black Grips 10 Round</span></span></strong></font></p> <p><span><span><font size="2"><em><span>Features vent rib barrel and adjustable rear sight. External hammer. Firing pin block safety. Magazine interlock with manual hold open. Button magazine release. Includes cable lanyard lock.</span></em></font><br></span></span></p> <p><font size="2">Phoenix Arms Model HP22 is a single action semi-auto .22LR caliber pistol with a staggered 10-round magazine that makes for a compact and comfortable fit in the hand. Weighing in at just 20 ounces in a size 4.1 by 5.5 inches, features include 3-inch vented rib barrel, serrated trigger, adjustable rear sight, magazine interlock with a manual slide hold open, external hammer and firing pin block safety. Available in satin nickel or matte black finish.
